Closes O
ticket O
20384 O
Add O
a O
one-word O
sentinel O
value O
of O
0x0 O
at O
the O
end O
of O
each O
buf_t O
chunk O
This O

where O

a O
buf_t O
memory O
is O

to O
a O

. O

Prevent O
a O

treating O
the O

of O
a O
buffer O
chunk O
as O

Vulnerability O
Details O
The O
Crosswalk O
Project O
, O
created O
by O
Intel O
s O
Open O
Source O

Center O
, O
allows O

. O

when O

invalid O
or O
self-signed O
SSL O
certificate O
is O
used O
during O
communication O
with O
the O
server O
, O

underlying O

this O
certificate O
. O

This O
behaviour O
could O
subject O
applications O
developed O
using O
this O
library O
to O
SSL O
MITM O
attacks O
. O

The O
project O
supports O
deployment O
to O
iOS O
, O
Windows O
Phone O
and O
Android O
. O

This O
applies O
even O
to O

over O
different O

and O
different O
certificates O
. O

This O
may O
allow O

attacker O
to O
mount O

attack O
using O
invalid O
SSL O
certificate O
and O

. O

: O

issue O
